tightening treatments?","acceptedAnswer":{"@type":"Answer","text":"Sofwave is unique in its use of SUPERB (Synchronous Ultrasound Parallel Beam) technology, which delivers focused ultrasound energy at a precise 1.5mm depth — the optimal zone for collagen stimulation in the mid-dermis. Unlike older ultrasound devices that target deeper tissue layers (which can be more painful), Sofwave concentrates energy exactly where it is most effective for skin tightening. Compared to RF-based devices, Sofwave achieves lifting and tightening through a different mechanism (ultrasound vs. radiofrequency), and many clinicians consider it complementary rather than competitive — which is why we offer both technologies at Rani Beauty Clinic."}},{"@type":"Question","name":"Is Sofwave painful?","acceptedAnswer":{"@type":"Answer","text":"Most patients describe Sofwave as very tolerable. You will feel brief bursts of warmth as the ultrasound energy is delivered, but the integrated Sofcool cooling system keeps the skin surface comfortable throughout. Pain tolerance varies, but the majority of patients complete the treatment without any numbing cream. For those with higher sensitivity, we can apply a topical anesthetic before the procedure. The discomfort level is significantly lower than many other skin tightening devices."}},{"@type":"Question","name":"How many Sofwave treatments do I need?","acceptedAnswer":{"@type":"Answer","text":"Most patients see meaningful results from a single Sofwave session. Clinical studies demonstrate significant improvement in skin laxity, fine lines, and wrinkles after one treatment. However, patients with more advanced laxity — particularly after significant weight loss — may benefit from a second session at 6–12 months or a combination protocol like The Reveal. Annual maintenance treatments can help sustain and build upon your results over time."}},{"@type":"Question","name":"Can Sofwave be combined with other treatments?","acceptedAnswer":{"@type":"Answer","text":"Yes, Sofwave pairs exceptionally well with other aesthetic treatments. For post-GLP-1 patients, our signature Reveal protocol strategically sequences Sofwave with Secret RF for comprehensive dual-layer skin restoration. Sofwave can also be performed alongside HydraFacial, chemical peels, and neurotoxin treatments as part of a comprehensive rejuvenation plan."}},{"@type":"Question","name":"How much does Sofwave cost?","acceptedAnswer":{"@type":"Answer","text":"Sofwave pricing depends on the treatment area. We also offer a Sofwave + RF Micro Combo package at $4,499 (1 Sofwave Full Face + 3 RF Micro Face sessions). For comprehensive post-weight-loss skin restoration, our Reveal protocol tiers start at $1,490. We accept HSA/FSA cards, and financing is available through Cherry and PatientFi with no credit impact."}},{"@type":"Question","name":"Is Sofwave effective for skin laxity after GLP-1 weight loss?","acceptedAnswer":{"@type":"Answer","text":"Sofwave is one of the most effective non-surgical options for addressing skin laxity after GLP-1 weight loss. When fat volume decreases rapidly — as often occurs with Ozempic, Wegovy, Mounjaro, or Zepbound — the skin's collagen network can't keep pace, resulting in loose, sagging skin. Sofwave directly stimulates new collagen and elastin production in the mid-dermis, helping the skin contract and tighten. For patients with more significant laxity, we recommend combining Sofwave with Secret RF in our Reveal protocol for dual-layer restoration."}},{"@type":"Question","name":"Can I get Sofwave while still taking my GLP-1 medication?","acceptedAnswer":{"@type":"Answer","text":"Yes. lg:py-28"><div class="mx-auto max-w-3xl px-6"><div style="opacity:0;transform:translateY(20px)"><div class="flex flex-col items-center gap-4 "><span class="font-body text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.15em] text-rani-gold">ABOUT THIS TREATMENT</span><div class="h-0.5 w-[60px] bg-rani-gold"></div></div><h2 class="mt-6 text-center font-body text-3xl font-bold text-rani-navy md:text-4xl">What Is <!-- -->Sofwave<!-- -->?</h2></div><div style="opacity:0;transform:translateY(20px)"><div class="mt-8 font-body text-base text-rani-text leading-relaxed whitespace-pre-line">Sofwave is an FDA-cleared, non-invasive ultrasound skin tightening device that uses proprietary Synchronous Ultrasound Parallel Beam (SUPERB) technology to treat fine lines, wrinkles, and skin laxity on the face, neck, and body. Unlike surgical facelifts, Sofwave delivers focused ultrasound energy at a precise depth of 1.5mm in the mid-dermis - the optimal zone for stimulating new collagen and elastin production.

The treatment works by creating controlled thermal zones beneath the skin&#x27;s surface while an integrated cooling mechanism protects the outer layer (epidermis) from damage. This triggers a natural wound-healing response that produces fresh, organized collagen over the following weeks and months, resulting in visibly tighter, smoother, and more lifted skin.

Sofwave is clinically proven to deliver results comparable to more invasive procedures without the risks, recovery time, or cost of surgery. It is safe for all skin types and tones (Fitzpatrick I-VI) and requires no anesthesia, incisions, or downtime.

At Rani Beauty Clinic, Sofwave is also a foundational component of The Reveal - our signature skin restoration protocol for patients experiencing skin changes after GLP-1 weight loss with medications like Ozempic, Wegovy, Mounjaro, and Zepbound. When combined with Secret RF microneedling in The Reveal protocol, Sofwave addresses deep collagen loss while RF targets surface texture - a dual-layer approach that no single technology achieves alone.</div></div></div></section><section class="bg-rani-cream py-12 md:py-20 lg:py-28"><div class="mx-auto max-w-4xl px-6"><div style="opacity:0;transform:translateY(20px)"><div class="flex flex-col items-center gap-4 "><span class="font-body text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.15em] text-rani-gold">THE PROCESS</span><div class="h-0.5 w-[60px] bg-rani-gold"></div></div><h2 class="mt-6 text-center font-body text-3xl font-bold text-rani-navy md:text-4xl">How It Works</h2></div><div class="mt-12 space-y-6" style="opacity:0"><div class="flex gap-6 rounded-xl bg-white p-6 shadow-[0_1px_3px_rgba(0,0,0,0.04)]" style="opacity:0;transform:translateY(20px)"><div class="flex h-10 w-10 shrink-0 items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-rani-navy text-white font-body font-bold text-sm">1</div><div><h3 class="font-body text-lg font-bold text-rani-navy">Consultation &amp; Assessment</h3><p class="mt-2 font-body text-sm text-rani-muted leading-relaxed">Your clinician evaluates your areas of concern - brow laxity, jowls, neck bands, fine lines, or post-weight-loss skin changes - and determines whether standalone Sofwave, a combination approach with RF microneedling, or our full Reveal protocol will achieve your goals most effectively.</p></div></div><div class="flex gap-6 rounded-xl bg-white p-6 shadow-[0_1px_3px_rgba(0,0,0,0.04)]" style="opacity:0;transform:translateY(20px)"><div class="flex h-10 w-10 shrink-0 items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-rani-navy text-white font-body font-bold text-sm">2</div><div><h3 class="font-body text-lg font-bold text-rani-navy">Treatment Preparation</h3><p class="mt-2 font-body text-sm text-rani-muted leading-relaxed">The treatment area is cleansed and a thin layer of ultrasound gel is applied. If you are currently on a GLP-1 medication, no adjustments are needed - Sofwave is fully compatible with active weight loss programs.</p></div></div><div style="opacity:0;transform:translateY(20px)"><div class="rounded-xl bg-white p-6 shadow-[0_1px_3px_rgba(0,0,0,0.04)] border-t-2 border-t-rani-gold"><h3 class="font-body text-lg font-bold text-rani-navy">During</h3><p class="mt-3 font-body text-sm text-rani-muted leading-relaxed">The treatment takes 30–90 minutes depending on the area treated. You will feel brief pulses of warmth as the ultrasound energy is delivered beneath the skin. The integrated cooling system keeps the surface comfortable. Most patients tolerate the treatment well without numbing.</p></div></div><div style="opacity:0;transform:translateY(20px)"><div class="rounded-xl bg-white p-6 shadow-[0_1px_3px_rgba(0,0,0,0.04)] border-t-2 border-t-rani-gold"><h3 class="font-body text-lg font-bold text-rani-navy">After</h3><p class="mt-3 font-body text-sm text-rani-muted leading-relaxed">You may experience mild redness, slight swelling, or tenderness in the treated area, which typically resolves within a few hours to a day. There is no peeling, bruising, or open wound. You can apply makeup, return to work, and resume all activities immediately. Avoid excessive heat (saunas, hot yoga) for 24–48 hours. Collagen remodeling begins immediately and continues building for 3–6 months.</p></div></div></div></div></section><section class="bg-white py-12 md:py-20 lg:py-28"><div class="mx-auto max-w-3xl px-6"><div style="opacity:0;transform:translateY(20px)"><div class="flex flex-col items-center gap-4 "><span class="font-body text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.15em] text-rani-gold">RESULTS</span><div class="h-0.5 w-[60px] bg-rani-gold"></div></div><h2 class="mt-6 text-center font-body text-3xl font-bold text-rani-navy md:text-4xl">Results &amp; Recovery</h2></div><div style="opacity:0;transform:translateY(20px)"><p class="mt-8 font-body text-base text-rani-text leading-relaxed">Initial tightening is often visible within 1–2 weeks as the skin responds to the thermal stimulation. The most significant results develop over 3–6 months as new collagen matures and remodels. Clinical studies show continued improvement for up to 12 months after a single treatment. Most patients achieve noticeable lifting and tightening from one session, though a second session at 6–12 months can amplify results. For post-GLP-1 patients with more significant laxity, combining Sofwave with Secret RF in our Reveal protocol delivers more comprehensive restoration than either treatment alone. Sofwave results are long-lasting because the new collagen is a permanent addition to your skin structure, though the natural aging process continues. Annual maintenance treatments help sustain your results.</p></div></div></section><section class="bg-rani-cream py-16 md:py-20"><div class="mx-auto max-w-4xl px-6"><div flex-col items-center gap-4 "><span class="font-body text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.15em] text-rani-gold">COMMON QUESTIONS</span><div class="h-0.5 w-[60px] bg-rani-gold"></div></div><h2 class="mt-6 text-center font-body text-3xl font-bold text-rani-navy md:text-4xl">Frequently Asked Questions</h2></div><div class="mt-12 space-y-4"><div style="opacity:0;transform:translateY(20px)"><details class="group rounded-xl border border-rani-border bg-white transition-all hover:shadow-sm"><summary class="flex cursor-pointer items-center justify-between px-6 py-4 font-body text-base font-semibold text-rani-navy">How is Sofwave different from other skin tightening treatments?<span class="ml-4 shrink-0 transition-transform duration-300 group-open:rotate-45 text-rani-gold text-xl">+</span></summary><div class="px-6 pb-4"><p class="font-body text-sm text-rani-muted leading-relaxed">Sofwave is unique in its use of SUPERB (Synchronous Ultrasound Parallel Beam) technology, which delivers focused ultrasound energy at a precise 1.5mm depth — the optimal zone for collagen stimulation in the mid-dermis. Unlike older ultrasound devices that target deeper tissue layers (which can be more painful), Sofwave concentrates energy exactly where it is most effective for skin tightening. Compared to RF-based devices, Sofwave achieves lifting and tightening through a different mechanism (ultrasound vs. radiofrequency), and many clinicians consider it complementary rather than competitive — which is why we offer both technologies at Rani Beauty Clinic.</p></div></details></div><div style="opacity:0;transform:translateY(20px)"><details class="group rounded-xl border border-rani-border bg-white transition-all hover:shadow-sm"><summary class="flex cursor-pointer items-center justify-between px-6 py-4 font-body text-base font-semibold text-rani-navy">Is Sofwave painful?<span class="ml-4 shrink-0 transition-transform duration-300 group-open:rotate-45 text-rani-gold text-xl">+</span></summary><div class="px-6 pb-4"><p class="font-body text-sm text-rani-muted leading-relaxed">Most patients describe Sofwave as very tolerable. You will feel brief bursts of warmth as the ultrasound energy is delivered, but the integrated Sofcool cooling system keeps the skin surface comfortable throughout. Pain tolerance varies, but the majority of patients complete the treatment without any numbing cream. For those with higher sensitivity, we can apply a topical anesthetic before the procedure. The discomfort level is significantly lower than many other skin tightening devices.</p></div></details></div><div style="opacity:0;transform:translateY(20px)"><details class="group rounded-xl border border-rani-border bg-white transition-all hover:shadow-sm"><summary class="flex cursor-pointer items-center justify-between px-6 py-4 font-body text-base font-semibold text-rani-navy">How many Sofwave treatments do I need?<span class="ml-4 shrink-0 transition-transform duration-300 group-open:rotate-45 text-rani-gold text-xl">+</span></summary><div class="px-6 pb-4"><p class="font-body text-sm text-rani-muted leading-relaxed">Most patients see meaningful results from a single Sofwave session. Clinical studies demonstrate significant improvement in skin laxity, fine lines, and wrinkles after one treatment. However, patients with more advanced laxity — particularly after significant weight loss — may benefit from a second session at 6–12 months or a combination protocol like The Reveal. Annual maintenance treatments can help sustain and build upon your results over time.</p></div></details></div><div style="opacity:0;transform:translateY(20px)"><details class="group rounded-xl border border-rani-border bg-white transition-all hover:shadow-sm"><summary class="flex cursor-pointer items-center justify-between px-6 py-4 font-body text-base font-semibold text-rani-navy">Can Sofwave be combined with other treatments?<span class="ml-4 shrink-0 transition-transform duration-300 group-open:rotate-45 text-rani-gold text-xl">+</span></summary><div class="px-6 pb-4"><p class="font-body text-sm text-rani-muted leading-relaxed">Yes, Sofwave pairs exceptionally well with other aesthetic treatments. At Rani Beauty Clinic, we offer a popular Sofwave + RF Microneedling combo package ($4,499) that combines the deep tissue tightening of Sofwave with the surface-level texture improvement of the Cutera Secret Pro. For post-GLP-1 patients, our signature Reveal protocol strategically sequences Sofwave with Secret RF for comprehensive dual-layer skin restoration. Sofwave can also be performed alongside HydraFacial, chemical peels, and neurotoxin treatments as part of a comprehensive rejuvenation plan.</p></div></details></div><div style="opacity:0;transform:translateY(20px)"><details class="group rounded-xl border border-rani-border bg-white transition-all hover:shadow-sm"><summary class="flex cursor-pointer items-center justify-between px-6 py-4 font-body text-base font-semibold text-rani-navy">How much does Sofwave cost?<span class="ml-4 shrink-0 transition-transform duration-300 group-open:rotate-45 text-rani-gold text-xl">+</span></summary><div class="px-6 pb-4"><p class="font-body text-sm text-rani-muted leading-relaxed">Sofwave pricing depends on the treatment area. A Brow Lift is $1,150, Lower Face (Jawline) is $2,250, Neck/Submental is $1,750, Full Face is $2,250, and Full Face + Neck is $3,999. We also offer a Sofwave + RF Micro Combo package at $4,499 (1 Sofwave Full Face + 3 RF Micro Face sessions). For comprehensive post-weight-loss skin restoration, our Reveal protocol tiers start at $1,490. We accept HSA/FSA cards, and financing is available through Cherry and PatientFi with no credit impact.</p></div></details></div><div style="opacity:0;transform:translateY(20px)"><details class="group rounded-xl border border-rani-border bg-white transition-all hover:shadow-sm"><summary class="flex cursor-pointer items-center justify-between px-6 py-4 font-body text-base font-semibold text-rani-navy">Is Sofwave effective for skin laxity after GLP-1 weight loss?<span class="ml-4 shrink-0 transition-transform duration-300 group-open:rotate-45 text-rani-gold text-xl">+</span></summary><div class="px-6 pb-4"><p class="font-body text-sm text-rani-muted leading-relaxed">Sofwave is one of the most effective non-surgical options for addressing skin laxity after GLP-1 weight loss. When fat volume decreases rapidly — as often occurs with Ozempic, Wegovy, Mounjaro, or Zepbound — the skin&#x27;s collagen network can&#x27;t keep pace, resulting in loose, sagging skin. Sofwave directly stimulates new collagen and elastin production in the mid-dermis, helping the skin contract and tighten. For patients with more significant laxity, we recommend combining Sofwave with Secret RF in our Reveal protocol for dual-layer restoration.</p></div></details></div><div style="opacity:0;transform:translateY(20px)"><details class="group rounded-xl border border-rani-border bg-white transition-all hover:shadow-sm"><summary class="flex cursor-pointer items-center justify-between px-6 py-4 font-body text-base font-semibold text-rani-navy">Can I get Sofwave while still taking my GLP-1 medication?<span class="ml-4 shrink-0 transition-transform duration-300 group-open:rotate-45 text-rani-gold text-xl">+</span></summary><div class="px-6 pb-4"><p class="font-body text-sm text-rani-muted leading-relaxed">Yes. There is no contraindication between Sofwave and GLP-1 medications including Semaglutide (Ozempic, Wegovy), Tirzepatide (Mounjaro, Zepbound), or Liraglutide. In fact, many providers recommend beginning skin tightening treatments before completing your weight loss journey. Starting Sofwave while still on your GLP-1 program gives your collagen a head start on remodeling, so your skin can better keep pace with continued fat loss.</p></div></details></div><div style="opacity:0;transform:translateY(20px)"><details class="group rounded-xl border border-rani-border bg-white transition-all hover:shadow-sm"><summary class="flex cursor-pointer items-center justify-between px-6 py-4 font-body text-base font-semibold text-rani-navy">What is The Reveal protocol and how does Sofwave fit in?<span class="ml-4 shrink-0 transition-transform duration-300 group-open:rotate-45 text-rani-gold text-xl">+</span></summary><div class="px-6 pb-4"><p class="font-body text-sm text-rani-muted leading-relaxed">The Reveal is Rani Beauty Clinic&#x27;s signature skin restoration protocol designed specifically for patients experiencing skin changes after GLP-1 weight loss. Sofwave serves as the deep-tightening component of The Reveal, working at 1.5mm depth to rebuild foundational collagen. Secret RF microneedling then addresses surface texture, pores, and superficial laxity. Together, they provide dual-layer restoration that no single device can achieve. The Reveal is available in three tiers (Essential, Signature, and Complete) with complimentary assessments.</p></div></details></div><div style="opacity:0;transform:translateY(20px)"><details class="group rounded-xl border border-rani-border bg-white transition-all hover:shadow-sm"><summary class="flex cursor-pointer items-center justify-between px-6 py-4 font-body text-base font-semibold text-rani-navy">How does Sofwave compare to a surgical facelift?<span class="ml-4 shrink-0 transition-transform duration-300 group-open:rotate-45 text-rani-gold text-xl">+</span></summary><div class="px-6 pb-4"><p class="font-body text-sm text-rani-muted leading-relaxed">Sofwave delivers meaningful lifting and tightening for patients with mild to moderate laxity without the risks, downtime, or cost of surgery. A surgical facelift remains the gold standard for severe laxity, but most patients — especially those in the early stages of post-weight-loss skin changes — achieve excellent results with Sofwave alone or in combination with RF microneedling. Sofwave requires no anesthesia, no incisions, and zero downtime. You can return to normal activities the same day.</p></div></details></div><div style="opacity:0;transform:translateY(20px)"><details class="group rounded-xl border border-rani-border bg-white transition-all hover:shadow-sm"><summary class="flex cursor-pointer items-center justify-between px-6 py-4 font-body text-base font-semibold text-rani-navy">What areas of the body can Sofwave treat?<span class="ml-4 shrink-0 transition-transform duration-300 group-open:rotate-45 text-rani-gold text-xl">+</span></summary><div class="px-6 pb-4"><p class="font-body text-sm text-rani-muted leading-relaxed">Sofwave is FDA-cleared for the face and neck, including the brow, full face, jawline, submentum (under chin), and neck. It is also used off-label for body areas including the upper arms, abdomen, and knees. At Rani Beauty Clinic, we offer Sofwave body tightening as part of our comprehensive approach to post-weight-loss skin restoration, particularly for patients in our Reveal protocol who want face and body treatment.</p></div></details></div></div></div></section><section class="bg-rani-cream py-12 md:py-20 lg:py-28"><div class="mx-auto max-w-4xl px-6"><div NAD+ is also a critical substrate for sirtuins - a family of protei"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"ns often called \"longevity genes\" - that regulate cellular aging, inflammation, and stress resistance.\n\nThe challenge is that NAD+ levels naturally decline with age - by the time you reach your 40s and 50s, your NAD+ levels may be half of what they were in your 20s. This decline is associated with many hallmarks of aging: decreased energy, cognitive decline, slower recovery, impaired DNA repair, and increased susceptibility to age-related diseases. Environmental stressors, chronic stress, poor sleep, and substance use can accelerate NAD+ depletion.\n\nNAD+ subcutaneous injections at Rani Beauty Clinic deliver NAD+ directly into the tissue just beneath the skin, where it is rapidly absorbed into the bloodstream. Unlike oral NAD+ supplements and precursors (like NMN and NR) that must be absorbed through the gut and converted through multiple metabolic steps, subcutaneous injection provides significantly higher bioavailability. The injection takes just minutes - making it a convenient, practical option for busy professionals who want the cellular benefits of NAD+ without dedicating hours to an IV session.2e:T656,Vitamin injections deliver essential vitamins, minerals, amino acids, and antioxidants directly into the muscle (intramuscular/IM) or bloodstream (intravenous/IV), bypassing the digestive system for significantly higher absorption rates compared to oral supplements. Injectable delivery ensures that 100% of the administered dose is available to your body.\n\nAt Rani Beauty Clinic, we offer a curated menu of the most impactful vitamin and nutrient injections, each selected for their evidence-based benefits and clinical utility.
